NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICE
DINAMALAR
(National Tamil Daily ESTD 1951)

Thiru R. Sathiamurthi erstwhile Partner of M/s. Dinamalar, has given a notice of Dissolution of Partnership Firm
M/s. Dinamalar, which is carrying on the business in Partnership in the running of Tamil Newspaper and allied weekly
supplements and yearly magazines under the name and style of Dinamalar, to the remaining Partners on 27th February 2012.
The dissolution of the said Partnership Firm, came into effect from 27th February 2012. This notice is given in accordance with
Section 73 of Indian Partnership Act, 1932.
Advertisement Marketing Office,
G-9, "C" Block,
Parsn Paradise Apartment,
109, G.N. Chetty Road,
T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017.
14th March 2012.

DR. R. VENKITAPATHY,
Partner, M/s. Dinamalar.
